<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pile</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijl.html>pijl</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pīlum</i>.

***pijler.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijler.html>pijler</a> (50958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijler.html>pijler</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pijlre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pilarium</i>, either directly or <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">piler</i>. The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pilaar.html>pilaar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> variant derived from the same source.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijler.html>pijler</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijlers.html>pijlers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijler.html>pijlertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a> (382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">poena</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">punishment, strife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ποινή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poinḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bloodmoney, weregild, fine, price paid, penalty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnen.html>pijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>physical pain, ache</li>
<li>psychological pain, hurt</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pīnus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tree</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***pijnappel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijnappel.html>pijnappel</a> (80407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Although the word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> formed very similarly to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pineapple</i>, their meanings now differ: the tropical fruit <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> instead known as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ananas.html>ananas</a></i> in modern Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnappel.html>pijnappel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnappels.html>pijnappels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnappel.html>pijnappeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pinecone <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dennenappel.html>dennenappel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">dennenkegel</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">pineapple</span> <span class="defdate">[17th to 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ananas.html>ananas</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnappel.html>pijnappel</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> houtige zaaddoos <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aantal.html>aantal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naaldbomen.html>naaldbomen</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnappel.html>pijnappel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> open <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omstandigheden.html>omstandigheden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gunstig.html>gunstig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaden.html>zaden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnboom.html>pijnboom</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnboom.html>pijnboom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnbomen.html>pijnbomen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnboom.html>pijnboompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pine, conifere of the genus <i>Pinus</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">den</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dennenboom.html>dennenboom</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">pinus</span></span></dd></dl>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pinigen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">pīnigon</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a great, painstaking effort</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijk.html>pijnlijk</a> (3322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijk.html>pijnlijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijker.html>pijnlijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijkst.html>pijnlijkst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>physically painful, inflicting bodily suffering</li>
<li>sore, pained</li>
<li>psychologically hurtful</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijk.html>pijnlijk</a></b>
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stillen.html>stillen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pik.html>pik</a> (1737)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pikken.html>pikken</a></i>. Compare the similar meanings in Scandinavian languages, e.g. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:pik.html>pik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bokm%C3%A5l" class="extiw" title="w:Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nb">pikk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pik.html>pik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pikken.html>pikken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pikje.html>pikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:smeekte.html>smeekte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pik.html>pik</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kontje.html>kontje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoppen.html>stoppen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I begged him to put his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>dick</a></b> back into my butthole.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A down, prejudiced attitude against someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thus 'picked on', especially from a position of authority</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> friend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Hé <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pik.html>pik</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorige.html>vorige</a> week <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gehad.html>gehad</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a></b>, have you <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> any <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> last week?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pic</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="duc">pec</i>. A variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pek.html>pek</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pitch <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">black material</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">picke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*pīk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*pīk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pickaxe, sharp point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***pil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pil.html>pil</a> (4952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pille</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pilla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pilula</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pila</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ball</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pil.html>pil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pillen.html>pillen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pilletje.html>pilletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a pill, an usually ball- or oval-shaped, coated portion of a drug to be <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> orally</li>
<li>(<i>with definite article: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pil.html>pil</a></b></i>) 'the' contraceptive pill
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:anticonceptiepil.html>anticonceptiepil</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>an analogous ball-shaped object</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an expert in pill use:
<ol><li>a pharmacist</li>
<li>an MD</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a med student</li></ol></li>
<li>a thick sandwich</li>
<li>a hard kick on a <a href = vnd.unilang:balk.html>balk</a> or other object</li>
<li>a bitter experience</li>
<li>a large book, a <a href = vnd.unilang:tomen.html>tome</a></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pile</i>.
</p>

***pilaf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pilaf.html>pilaf</a> (101316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">pilav</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">پلاو</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pelâv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">पुलाव</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pulāv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">पुलाक</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pulāka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dravidian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Dravidian languages">Dravidian</a></span> origin. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pilaf.html>pilaf</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pilafs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A dish made by browning grain, typically rice, in oil and then cooking it with a seasoned broth, to which meat and/or vegetables may be added.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">pilot</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">pillot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">piloto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pillottus</i>; perhaps ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πηδόν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pēdón</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blade of an oar, oar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pimpernel.html>pimpernel</a> (68046)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pimpernel.html>pimpernel</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

***pinata.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pinata.html>pinata</a> (44854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Mexican <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">piñata</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">piña</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pinea</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pinecone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, because its paper cover (on traditional making) resembles one. Alternatively from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">pignatta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> from a Chinese custom allegedly introduced by <a href = vnd.unilang:marco.html>Marco</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:polo.html>Polo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinata.html>pinata</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinatas.html>pinatas</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Latin American culture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A doll or other decorated container that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> filled with candy and hit with a hammer or a stick by blindfolded children during birthday parties or other celebrations until the candy falls out.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinata.html>pinata</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinatas.html>pinatas</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pinataing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pinataed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To hit something or someone with <a href = vnd.unilang:sticks.html>sticks</a> after having filled them with candy.
<ul><li>2015 (November 20) "<a href = vnd.unilang:zombie.html>Zombie</a> Broheims", episode 14 of Pig Goat Banana Cricket
<dl><dd>Cricket: "Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pinata.html>pinata</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!"</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***pinball.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pinball.html>pinball</a> (35735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pin</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ball</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinball.html>pinball</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pinballs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A game, played on a device with a sloping base, in which the player operates a spring-loaded plunger to shoot a ball, between obstacles, and attempts to hit targets and score points.</li>
<li>The ball used in <a href = vnd.unilang:pinball.html>pinball</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> soccer</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A situation where a ball <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> frantically kicked between many players.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> January 15,  Saj Chowdhury,  “Man City 4 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 3 Wolves”, in  <cite>BBC</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/9357962.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The opener <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> from a Jarvis ball which struck Aleksandar Kolarov <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> route to a lively round of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pinball.html>pinball</a></b> between City players before it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> poked in by Milijas.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinball.html>pinball</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">pinballs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pinballing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pinballed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To dart about rapidly.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1996</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> Applebome,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:dixie.html>Dixie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>Rising</a>: How the South <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Shaping American Values, Politics and Culture</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Like most immigrants, Gibbs <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> South for economic reasons and soon found himself <b>pinballing</b> around a world circumscribed by the hot growth markets...</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  David Baldacci,  <cite>Hour Game</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">They <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> off the road and <b>pinballed</b> alongside a stretch of guardrail as the Bambis scattered.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pincet.html>pincet</a> (25201)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">pincette</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tweezers; poker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pincet.html>pincet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pincetten.html>pincetten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pincet.html>pincetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pair of tweezers, small (usually metal) pincers, used for handling small <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> and in medicine</li></ol>

***pinda.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pinda.html>pinda</a> (14320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Papiamento" class="extiw" title="w:Papiamento">Papiamentu</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pap"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinda.html>pinda</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kongo_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kongo language"><a href = vnd.unilang:kongo.html>Kongo</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kg">mpinda</i>; see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pinder</i>. Sense 4 <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from the pejorative term <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">pindachinees</i> from the 1930s, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> applied <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> more pejoratively to people from East Asia in general, including Indonesians who <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> masse to the Netherlands in the late 1940s.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinda.html>pinda</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinda.html>pinda</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pindaatje.html>pindaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a peanut, the nut-like pod containing the edible seed(s) of a leguminous plant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pinda.html>Pinda</a>'s</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:groeien.html>groeien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:peanuts.html>Peanuts</a> grow underground</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the annual herb <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Arachnis_hypogea" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Arachnis hypogea"><i>Arachnis hypogea</i></a></span>, which produces the above</li>
<li><span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> the above seeds, gathered to be eaten as a snack or processed into food products</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ethnic slur</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> people from East Asia, most commonly Chinese and Indonesians</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardnoot.html>aardnoot</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aardpimpernoot</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">apennoot</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">grondnoot</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">Lombokker</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">olienoot</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">piendel</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cognate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pinda.html>pinda</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:plantkunde.html>plantkunde</a>)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Arachis_hypogaea" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Arachis hypogaea"><span style="color:green;"><i>Arachis hypogaea</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vlinderbloemenfamilie <a href = vnd.unilang:behorende.html>behorende</a> plant</li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrucht.html>vrucht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> plant</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pindakaas.html>pindakaas</a> (7553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinda.html>pinda</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peanut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaas.html>kaas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheese, paste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The compound originates from Suriname, where it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> possibly used as early as the late eighteenth century.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pindakaas.html>pindakaas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pindakaas.html>pindakazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pindakaas.html>pindakaasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>peanut butter <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a spread made from ground <a href = vnd.unilang:peanuts.html>peanuts</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***pingelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pingelen.html>pingelen</a> (53517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:pingelen.html>pingel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small item</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">ping(-ping)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">money</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; if so, cognate with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">pinkelen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pinch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pinch</i>) and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pimpelen.html>pimpel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small glass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also "blue tit."
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pingelen.html>pingelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wrangle, to try to get a better price.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afdingen.html>afdingen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjacheren.html>sjacheren</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">makelen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marchanderen.html>marchanderen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do fine needlework</li></ol>
